Add 4 more BP_Couch as park benches ---\ndef is_clear(x, y, z, min_dist=250):\n    for a in eas.get_all_level_actors():\n        try:\n            l = a.get_actor_location()\n            if abs(l.x) > 1e7: continue\n            dx, dy = l.x - x, l.y - y\n            if dx*dx + dy*dy < min_dist*min_dist:\n                return False\n        except: pass\n    return True\n\ndef ground_z(x, y, default_z):\n    try:\n        pt = unreal.NavigationSystemV1.project_point_to_navigation(world, unreal.Vector(x, y, default_z))\n        if pt and hasattr(pt,'x') and (pt.x or pt.y or pt.z):\n            return pt.z\n    except: pass\n    return default_z\n\nps_z = unreal.GameplayStatics.get_all_actors_of_class(world, unreal.PlayerStart)[0].get_actor_location().z\ncouch_bp = unreal.load_object(None, \"/Game/CityDatabase/blueprints/BP_Couch.BP_Couch_C\")\nbench_positions = [(600, 0), (-600, 0), (0, 700), (0, -700)]\ncouches_added = 0\nfor i, (x, y) in enumerate(bench_positions):\n    if not is_clear(x, y, ps_z, 220): continue\n    z = ground_z(x, y, ps_z)\n    if couch_bp:\n        a = eas.spawn_actor_from_class(couch_bp, unreal.Vector(x, y, z))\n        if a: a.set_actor_label(f\"ParkBench_{i}\"); couches_added += 1\nprint(f\"COUCHES_ADDED={couches_added}\")\n\n# --- 5. Add 4 more trash bins at park paths ---\ntrash_bp = unreal.load_object(None, \"/Game/CityDatabase/blueprints/BP_Trash_bin_a.BP_Trash_bin_a_C\")\ntrash_positions = [(800, 0), (-800, 0), (0, 800), (0, -800)]\ntrash_added = 0\nfor i, (x, y) in enumerate(trash_positions):\n    if not is_clear(x, y, ps_z, 200): continue\n    z = ground_z(x, y, ps_z)\n    if trash_bp:\n        a = eas.spawn_actor_from_class(trash_bp, unreal.Vector(x, y, z))\n        if a: a.set_actor_label(f\"ParkTrashBin_{i}\"); trash_added += 1\nprint(f\"TRASH_ADDED={trash_added}\")\n"}}
